<Text>The Taco Shack Restaurant- located in the historical Inland Empire community of Redlands,California is a great place to relax and enjoy great Mexican Cuisine with a healthy twist! They have a sparkling clean "A" rated restaurant to either eat in or convenient take-away to go orders as well!
They serve breakfast,lunch and dinners at The Taco Shack!
What really sets The Taco Shack apart from others is their freshly made tacos,tostadas,rellenos,burritos,chips,salsa bar and menudo using low salt ingredients and very fresh carne asada,al pastor,grilled chicken,ground beef,pork and vegetarian selections as well!They have delicious nacho plates that are a meal in themselves and great appetizers to start off your meal!
They also feature a classic taco salad with tasty low salt,low fat refried beans,guacamole,fresh lettuce,delicious freshly shredded cheese,your choice of meats (or no meat vegeterian!) all in a fresh and tasty flour tortilla bowl-this was super tasty! They also serve fresh fruit dishes and have a selection of deserts to complete your meal.
They have self serve soft drinks by Pepsi,horchatas,orange whip,as well as imported from Mexico bottled beverages along with a nice selection of beer from the fridge!
The servers are very friendly,courteous and offer selection suggestions for you.
The food is served promptly and is a great value for the fresh and tasty portions that you receive!
Lots of free parking and family friendly.
I had a great eating experience at The Taco Shack,Redlands,California and I would highly recommend them to anyone interested in great and healthy Mexican cuisine!
.
.
.

I have a dress!!! I was having the hardest time finding a knee- or tea-length white dress that still looked bridal. I was thrilled to find such a good selection at Simply Bridal. Luckily, I live close to their showroom and was able to visit twice in person to try on some options. I was immediately impressed by the quality of the dresses for the price. After my first appointment, they helped me make a second one so I could return with my mom and sister to make a final decision. One of the great things about dresses at Simply Bridal is that many of their short dresses are actually bridesmaid dresses in white (with no markup!). I can't express how thrilled I was to find a place like Simply Bridal. Highly recommended!</text>

<Text>Nice to have a Great tasting Korean BBQ chicken place nearby. I believe to get anything of this quality, you would need to live more towards Korea town or the San Gabriel Valley. This review is based on two of my visits during the While Covid ordeal. I want to first cover how easy it is to order either on the phone or online. Keep note that if you do try ordering online they do have 10% off during this review for first time users. Ordering is really easy either on the phone or online. Everything is pretty self explanatory, and you could even write some notes there if you wish to alter an order. There is Apple Pay, and they will notify you by text that your order is ready, so you don‚Äôt really need to wait around. Super convenient, to get your food and get out.

Food
I have tried the whole chicken (you can pick two versions) we tried the golden chicken and the secret spicy. The Secret spicy is SO good. The only sauce I have tried so far that I wasn‚Äôt a big fan of, was the honey garlic, I believe it had a bit too much garlic. The kimchi fried rice was mediocre in my opinion, and to note, the fries are the steak fries.

Things I would recommend :
Soy Garlic Wings- these are BURSTING with flavor. You just gotta get these, and you will easily come back for more.

So the second time I went back, I had to order the wings again, and I have yet to try the other things on the menu. Goal is also to try the Duk Bukki as I am a fan of rice cakes. I hope I made it easier for anyone that was considering this place, I hope to update my review soon on other items. Until then!< /Text></record></dataset><record>

<Review>While it's not "authentic" Mexican food, it's an okay substitue. Like store-bought sushi vs. restaurant.
For the 10 years Adalberto's has been part of my regular diet I have no real complaints about the food. However, compared with a genuine taqueria , the meals definitely lack in flavor complexity.
The cost is fair and the service is 24 hours; so they're that always-on service that is hard to find in the restaurant industry. Be advised, 3am orders take a considerable amount of waiting time out at the drive-through window. At least they're probably making sure it's all heated to correct temperature.
I would give 4 stars, but customer service here is pretty much shitt; so 3 seems fair.< /Review>< date>

<Date>1598821767837</Date><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
For those craving the flavor of SoCal Mexican food, with crispy rolled tacos with guac, big cheesy bean burritos, machaca, crispy fried tacos, and some simple good spicy red or green hot sauce, this chain is the only one in my 20+ years living and searching in northern CA that truly pushes all those buttons. It is NOT like what you get at any other Mexican joint in NorCal. You will not get a super burrito with rice and lettuce on it. You will NOT get soft tiny street tacos where the fillings fall out if you don't use all your fingers to pinch it together. You WILL get deliciously cheesy and crispy satisfying food at a reasonable price.< /Text>
